    <div id="office-StandaloneSKU-awqtjuw" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;officeStandaloneSKU 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_office-StandaloneSKU&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m4r3a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r3a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR2|coreui-region|office-StandaloneSKU-awqtjuw|office-StandaloneSKU"> 
     <div data-module="ow-standalone-sku" data-grid="container" class="ow-padding-0" data-layout="ow-default">

       <div class="ow-standalone-sku-left ow-sku-center-align">

          <h3>Looking for Office as a one-time purchase?</h3>

        <div class="ow-display-ib ow-theme-microsoft365"> <a href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-365/get-started-with-office-2019#compare_table" class="c-button f-primary ow-mv-0010 ow-mh-0005" aria-label="Compare Office 2019 products" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CompareProducts&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;n1m4r3a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m4r3a2&quot;,&quot;tags&quot;:{&quot;BiLinkName&quot;:&quot;CompareProducts&quot;}}" role="button"> <span>Compare products</span> </a> 
        </div>

       <div class="ow-standalone-sku-right">

         </div>

    </div> 
    <div id="office-CustomSpacingTemplate-1kr8qn7" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;r2Spacer 4&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_office-CustomSpacingTemplate&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m5r3a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r3a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR2|coreui-region|office-CustomSpacingTemplate-1kr8qn7|office-CustomSpacingTemplate"> 
     <div aria-hidden="true" class="ow-m-cstm-spcng x-clearfix" data-module="ow-custom-spacing"> 
      <div class="ow-spacer ow-mobile-spacer ow-theme-light ow-theme-bg" data-grid="col-12" style="padding-bottom: 25px;"></div> 
      <div class="ow-spacer ow-desktop-spacer ow-theme-light ow-theme-bg" data-grid="col-12" style="padding-bottom: 25px;"></div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div id="office-CustomSpacingTemplate-0fc3wzy" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;r2Spacer 2&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_office-CustomSpacingTemplate&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m6r3a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r3a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR2|coreui-region|office-CustomSpacingTemplate-0fc3wzy|office-CustomSpacingTemplate"> 
     <div aria-hidden="true" class="ow-m-cstm-spcng x-clearfix" data-module="ow-custom-spacing"> 
      <div class="ow-spacer ow-mobile-spacer" data-grid="col-12" style="padding-bottom: 25px;"></div> 
      <div class="ow-spacer ow-desktop-spacer" data-grid="col-12" style="padding-bottom: 25px;"></div> 
     </div>

   </div> 
   <div id="primaryR3" data-grid="container" data-region-key="primaryr3" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;primaryR3 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Region_coreui-region&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;a2&quot;}"> 
    <div id="coreui-heading-qwkoeun" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;R3Heading 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-heading&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR3|coreui-region|coreui-heading-qwkoeun|coreui-heading"> 
     <header role="presentation" class="m-heading-2"> 
      <h2 class="c-heading-3">Frequently asked questions</h2> 
     </header> 
    </div> 
    <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;CollapseDrawer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR3|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
     <section class="cui-drawer"> 
      <div class="cui-header f-divider"> 
       <div class="cui-drawer-toggle"> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Expand all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="f-expand c-action-toggle" name="Expand all" data-toggled-label="Expand all" aria-label="Expand all">Expand all</button> <span>|</span> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Collapse all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="f-collapse c-action-toggle" name="Collapse all" data-toggled-label="Collapse all" aria-label="Collapse all" disabled>Collapse all</button> 
       </div> 
       <div style="clear: both;"></div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer0">What is Microsoft 365?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft 365 is the productivity cloud designed to help each of us achieve what matters, in our work and life, with best-in-class Office apps, intelligent cloud services, and advanced security.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer1">What happened to Office 365 business plans?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Office 365 business plans are now Microsoft 365 business plans. New name, same great value, same price.</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Office 365 Business Essentials is now Microsoft 365 Business Basic</li> 
         <li>Office 365 Business Premium is now Microsoft 365 Business Standard</li> 
         <li>Microsoft 365 Business is now Microsoft 365 Business Premium</li> 
         <li>Office 365 Business is now Microsoft 365 Apps for business</li> 
        </ul> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer2">Why did you change the name from Office 365 to Microsoft 365?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>We changed the name to be more reflective of the range of features and benefits in the subscription. Microsoft 365 includes everything you know in Office 365, including best-in-class Office apps, intelligent cloud services, and advanced security.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer3">Where business plan names have changed, has the product or price changed?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>There are no price or feature changes for small and medium business plans. The same plans are available, only with an updated name.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn7m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:7,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer4">My business has an existing Office 365 business subscription. What does the change to Microsoft 365 mean for me?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer4" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>No action is needed from you. Your Office 365 subscription will automatically be renamed to Microsoft 365. You will see the name of your subscription update to the new name across your Admin Portal and monthly billing statements.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn8m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:8,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer5">How many devices can I install Office apps on if I have a Microsoft 365 business plan?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer5" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Subscribers can install Office apps on up to five PCs or Macs, five tablets, and five mobile devices. You can count hybrid Windows devices, such as the Microsoft Surface Pro, as either a PC or a tablet.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn9m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:9,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer6">What forms of payment can I use?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer6" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>You can pay with all major credit cards, and your subscription amount will appear on your credit card statement. For Microsoft 365 business plans, you have the option to receive an invoice and, depending on your choice of services, you will be billed monthly or annually. You receive an email message when your invoice is ready to be viewed and, if a purchase order number is entered when you buy your subscription, that number is included in your invoice.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn10m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:10,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer7">What’s the difference between monthly, annual, and annual commitment payments?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer7" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>To provide customers with the greatest amount of flexibility, different payment options are available.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>Microsoft 365 Business Basic, Apps for business, Business Standard, and Business Premium plans are available for monthly commitment payment or annual commitment payment.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Monthly commitment payment: You pay month by month, and you can cancel at any time.</li> 
         <li>Annual commitment payment: You sign up for a one-year subscription, but you can choose to pay month to month or pay for the entire year at the time you sign up. There is a discount for using this payment option.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>The Microsoft 365 Enterprise and Office 365 Enterprise plans (including standalone plans such as Exchange Online) and Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise are available for annual commitment payment.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Annual commitment payment: You sign up for a one-year subscription, but you can choose to pay month to month or pay for the entire year at the time you sign up.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn11m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:11,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer8">Can I convert my trial to a paid subscription and retain all my settings and files?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer8" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Yes. If you purchase Microsoft 365 licenses for the accounts you create during your free trial, the information and configuration for these users' accounts will remain intact. Once your free trial expires, you will have an additional 30 days to purchase Microsoft 365 before your account information is erased. Once your trial account information has been erased, it cannot be retrieved.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn12m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:12,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer9">Does Microsoft 365 work when I am not connected to the internet?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer9" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>The Office apps that you install on your PC or Mac such as Word, Excel, PowerPoint and Outlook are available to you when you are not online.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>With OneDrive in Microsoft 365, you get file storage that you can access when offline. When you make changes while offline, they will be sync’d to OneDrive and across the rest of your devices when you reconnect.</p> 
        <p>&nbsp;</p> 
        <p>With Outlook, you can read emails already delivered to your inbox or draft new emails and meeting requests. Your inbox and outbox will sync across the rest of your devices when you reconnect.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn13m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:13,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer10">What happens to my data if I cancel my subscription?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer10" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Your data is yours. If you decide to cancel your Microsoft 365 subscription, you can download your data—for example, your email and documents on team sites—and save it to another location. You should save your data before you cancel. After you cancel your subscription, data associated with your Microsoft 365 account will be available to your administrator(s) in a limited function account for 90 days.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer f-divider"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn14m2r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:14,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r4a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer11">Where can I find even more answers to frequently asked questions?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-s3dgqka-collapsible-drawer11" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>You can find more answers to frequently asked questions on our <a aria-label="Microsoft 365 for business FAQ page" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-365/business/microsoft-365-frequently-asked-questions" class="c-hyperlink">Microsoft 365 for business FAQ page</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </section> 
    </div> 
    <div id="coreui-contentrichblock-lni8j9r" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;r3contentrichblock 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contentrichblock&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m3r4a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r4a2&quot;}" data-module-id="DepartmentPage|primaryR3|coreui-region|coreui-contentrichblock-lni8j9r|coreui-contentrichblock">

For complete requirements for PC and Mac see <a aria-label="See full system requirements" href="https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-365/microsoft-365-and-office-resources" class="c-hyperlink">system requirements</a>.<br> 2. For HD calling, compatible HD hardware and broadband connection with at least 4 Mbps required.<br> 3. This plan works with Office 2019, Office 2016, and Office 2013. Previous versions of Office, such as Office 2010, may work with Microsoft&nbsp;365 with reduced functionality. This compatibility with Office does not include the Office 365 F3&nbsp;plans.<br> 4.&nbsp;After your 1-month free trial, you will be charged the applicable subscription fee. Credit card required.
